Each DSL operation is backed by a ProcessorSupplier that creates Processor instances:\\n\\n### KStream Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>\\n   - Implements the Predicate logic for filtering records\\n   - Inner class KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n\\n2. **KStreamMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java)\\n   - Kafka Streams codebase provides a clear separation between the high-level DSL (Domain Specific Language) and the lower-level Processor API implementation. This separation is essential for teams migrating from the DSL to the Processor API for custom state store management.\\n\\n## DSL Layer\\n\\nThe primary DSL implementation classes are:\\n\\n1. **KStreamImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java) - The core implementation of the KStream DSL interface. Key DSL methods include:\\n   - `filter(Predicate)` - Filters records based on a predicate\\n   - `map(KeyValueMapper)` - Transforms both keys and values\\n   - `mapValues(ValueMapperWithKey)` - Transforms only values\\n   - `groupBy(KeyValueMapper)` - Groups records by a new key\\n   - `groupByKey()` - Groups records by their existing key\\n\\n2. **KTableImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableImpl.java) - The implementation of the KTable (changelog stream) DSL interface with similar operations optimized for changelog semantics.\\n\\n3. **KGroupedStreamImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KGroupedStreamImpl.java) - The implementation of KGroupedStream, representing the result of groupBy operations. It provides aggregation methods like `reduce()`, `count()`, and `aggregate()`.\\n\\n## Processor API Layer\\n\\nThe Processor API provides the low-level implementation details. Each DSL operation is backed by a ProcessorSupplier that creates Processor instances:\\n\\n### KStream Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>\\n   - Implements the Predicate logic for filtering records\\n   - Inner class KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n\\n2. **KStreamMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java)\\n   - Implements ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>\\n   - Applies KeyValueMapper to transform both keys and values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Accesses the Processor API context() to forward transformed records\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>\\n   - Applies ValueMapperWithKey to transform only values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n   - Uses FixedKeyRecord for records with unchanged keys\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMap.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMap but produces multiple output records per input\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMapValues.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMapValues but produces multiple output records\\n\\n### KTable Processors:\\n\\n1. **KTableFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableFilter.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>\\n   - Processes Change<VIn> records (changelog entries)\\n   - Handles state store management for materialized views\\n   - Inner class KTableFilterProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VIn>>\\n\\n2. **KTableMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>\\n   - Processes Change records with state store support\\n   - Handles both old and new values for changelog semantics\\n   - Inner class KTableMapValuesProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VOut>>\\n\\n### Aggregation Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamAggregate** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamAggregate.java)\\n   - Implements KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>\\n   - Used by KGroupedStream for aggregation operations\\n   - Manages state stores for accumulating aggregate values\\n   - Inner class KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Processes records and maintains aggregate state\\n\\n## Integration Pattern\\n\\nThe migration pattern from DSL to Processor API follows this flow:\\n\\n1. DSL method call (e.g., `stream.filter(predicate)`) in KStreamImpl\\n2. Creates a ProcessorParameters with the corresponding Processor supplier\\n3. Processor supplier (e.g., KStreamFilter) implements ProcessorSupplier interface\\n4. Processor supplier's `get()` method returns a Processor instance\\n5. The Processor implements the actual logic, accessing ProcessorContext for:\\n   - Forwarding records downstream: `context().forward(record)`\\n   - Accessing state stores (for stateful operations)\\n   - Managing timestamps and metadata\\n\\n## Key Processor API Interfaces:\\n\\n- **ProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java) - Factory for creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java) - Specialized supplier for fixed-key operations\\n- **Processor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java) - Base interface for all processors\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessor.java) - Specialized processor for operations that don't change keys\\n\\nTeams migrating from DSL to Processor API can leverage these implementations as reference patterns for custom state store management, replacing the DSL convenience with direct Processor API control over store initialization, record processing, and forwarding logic.\"\n   189→}\n   190→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. \"KStreamAggregate\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Apache Kafka Streams codebase provides a clear separation between the high-level DSL (Domain Specific Language) and the lower-level Processor API implementation. This separation is essential for teams migrating from the DSL to the Processor API for custom state store management.\\n\\n## DSL Layer\\n\\nThe primary DSL implementation classes are:\\n\\n1. **KStreamImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java) - The core implementation of the KStream DSL interface. Key DSL methods include:\\n   - `filter(Predicate)` - Filters records based on a predicate\\n   - `map(KeyValueMapper)` - Transforms both keys and values\\n   - `mapValues(ValueMapperWithKey)` - Transforms only values\\n   - `groupBy(KeyValueMapper)` - Groups records by a new key\\n   - `groupByKey()` - Groups records by their existing key\\n\\n2. **KTableImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableImpl.java) - The implementation of the KTable (changelog stream) DSL interface with similar operations optimized for changelog semantics.\\n\\n3. **KGroupedStreamImpl** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KGroupedStreamImpl.java) - The implementation of KGroupedStream, representing the result of groupBy operations. It provides aggregation methods like `reduce()`, `count()`, and `aggregate()`.\\n\\n## Processor API Layer\\n\\nThe Processor API provides the low-level implementation details. Each DSL operation is backed by a ProcessorSupplier that creates Processor instances:\\n\\n### KStream Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFilter.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>\\n   - Implements the Predicate logic for filtering records\\n   - Inner class KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n\\n2. **KStreamMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMap.java)\\n   - Implements ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>\\n   - Applies KeyValueMapper to transform both keys and values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Accesses the Processor API context() to forward transformed records\\n\\n3. **KStreamMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>\\n   - Applies ValueMapperWithKey to transform only values\\n   - Inner class KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor\\n   - Uses FixedKeyRecord for records with unchanged keys\\n\\n4. **KStreamFlatMap** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMap.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMap but produces multiple output records per input\\n\\n5. **KStreamFlatMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamFlatMapValues.java)\\n   - Similar pattern to KStreamMapValues but produces multiple output records\\n\\n### KTable Processors:\\n\\n1. **KTableFilter** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableFilter.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>\\n   - Processes Change<VIn> records (changelog entries)\\n   - Handles state store management for materialized views\\n   - Inner class KTableFilterProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VIn>>\\n\\n2. **KTableMapValues** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KTableMapValues.java)\\n   - Implements KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>\\n   - Processes Change records with state store support\\n   - Handles both old and new values for changelog semantics\\n   - Inner class KTableMapValuesProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VOut>>\\n\\n### Aggregation Processors:\\n\\n1. **KStreamAggregate** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamAggregate.java)\\n   - Implements KStreamAggProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VAgg>\\n   - Used by KGroupedStream for aggregation operations\\n   - Manages state stores for accumulating aggregate values\\n   - Inner class KStreamAggregateProcessor extends ContextualProcessor\\n   - Processes records and maintains aggregate state\\n\\n## Integration Pattern\\n\\nThe migration pattern from DSL to Processor API follows this flow:\\n\\n1. DSL method call (e.g., `stream.filter(predicate)`) in KStreamImpl\\n2. Creates a ProcessorParameters with the corresponding Processor supplier\\n3. Processor supplier (e.g., KStreamFilter) implements ProcessorSupplier interface\\n4. Processor supplier's `get()` method returns a Processor instance\\n5. The Processor implements the actual logic, accessing ProcessorContext for:\\n   - Forwarding records downstream: `context().forward(record)`\\n   - Accessing state stores (for stateful operations)\\n   - Managing timestamps and metadata\\n\\n## Key Processor API Interfaces:\\n\\n- **ProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java) - Factory for creating Processor instances\\n- **FixedKeyProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java) - Specialized supplier for fixed-key operations\\n- **Processor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java) - Base interface for all processors\\n- **FixedKeyProcessor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/FixedKeyProcessor.java) - Specialized processor for operations that don't change keys\\n\\nTeams migrating from DSL to Processor API can leverage these implementations as reference patterns for custom state store management, replacing the DSL convenience with direct Processor API control over store initialization, record processing, and forwarding logic.\"\n}\n","numLines":190,"startLine":1,"totalLines":190}}}
